  <script type="text/javascript">
   /* <![CDATA[ */
var pmc_krux = {"lob":"rollingstone","page-type":"home","env":"desktop","primary-category":"","primary-vertical":"","vertical":"","category":"","tag":"","author":"","logged-in":"no","subscriber-type":"free"};

  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var pmc = pmc || {};
		pmc.subscription_v2 = pmc.subscription_v2 || {};

		/**
		 * Extend pmc global to get subscriber data.
		 */
		pmc.subscription_v2 = {
			is_paywall_content: true,

			is_single_post: false,

			is_admin_user: false,

			is_token_user: false,

			iframe_refresh_token_id: 'iframe_refresh_token',

			ajax_url: "https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",

			login_link: "https://api.pmc.com/authorization/login?returnTo=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.rollingstone.com%2F&brand=rs&source=website",

			is_ip_auth_enabled: true,

			subscriber_data: {},

			brands: {
				'variety-vip': 'vy',
				'rs': 'rs',
				'wwd': 'wwd',
				'sportico': 'sportico'
			},

			brand_name: "rs",

			/**
			 * A queue of listeners that will fire when subscriber data is loaded.
			 */
			subscriber_data_listeners: [],

			render_links_from_theme: false,

			/**
			 * Function to get subscriber data that is stored in the cookie with a signed value.
			 * @param {function} callback
			 * @return {void}
			 */
			get_cookie_data: function (callback) {
				var self   = pmc.subscription_v2;
				var url    = self.ajax_url;
				var params = '?action=pmc_get_cookie_data_ajax_callback';
				var xhr    = self.get_xhr_get(url, params);

				// Setup our listener to process completed requests
				xhr.onload = function () {
					callback && callback(JSON.parse(xhr.response), xhr.status);
				};

				xhr.send();
			},

			/**
			* Generate a random string.
			*
			* @return {string}
			*/
			get_random: function () {
				return Math.random().toString( 36 ).substring( 2, 15 ) + Math.random().toString( 36 ).substring( 2, 15 );
			},

			/**
			 * Do ajax call to refresh token of the current session
			 *
			 * @param {object} event
			 * @return {void}
			 */
			listen_for_refresh_iframe_postmessage: function(event) {
				// Do nothing if we don't have data
				if ( ! event.data ) {
					return;
				}

				var authApiOrigin = "https://api.pmc.com";

				// Bail if this postMessage originated elsewhere
				if ( authApiOrigin !== event.origin ) {
					return;
				}

				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;
				var destroyIframe = false;
				var jsonParseError = false;

				try {
					var data = JSON.parse(event.data);
				} catch(error) {
					var data = event.data;
					jsonParseError = true;
					Rollbar.warn('Failed to parse response from Auth API', {data: data, session: self.get_session_data() });
				}

				if( false === jsonParseError && ! data.hasOwnProperty('jwt') ) {
					Rollbar.warn('Unexpected token refresh data returned from Auth API', {data: data, session: self.get_session_data() });
				}

				if( '' === data.jwt ){
					switch (data.message) {
						// Remove user session if Auth0 has done the same
						case 'login_required':
							var url    = self.ajax_url;
							var params = '?action=pmc_delete_subscriber_session_cookie_callback';
							var xhr    = self.get_xhr_get(url, params);

							xhr.send();

							destroyIframe = true;

							Rollbar.info('login_required returned from Auth API', {data: data, session: self.get_session_data()});
							break;
						// Auth API revokes IP authed session and returns `site_license_mismatch` when IP got changed
						case 'site_license_mismatch':
							var url    = self.ajax_url;
							var params = '?action=pmc_delete_subscriber_cookie_ajax_callback';
							var xhr    = self.get_xhr_get(url, params);

							xhr.send();

							destroyIframe = true;
							MicroModal.show( 'pmc-subscription__site-license-mismatch-modal' );

							Rollbar.info('site_license_mismatch returned from Auth API', {data: data, session: self.get_session_data()});
							break;
						default:
							if ( false === jsonParseError ) {
								Rollbar.warn( 'Unexpected token refresh message returned from Auth API',
									{ data: data, session: self.get_session_data() } );
							}
							break;
					}

				}

				// Save new user data
				if ( data.jwt && 'success' === data.message ) {
					var url    = self.ajax_url;
					var params = '?action=token_refresh_ajax_callback' + '&jwt=' + data.jwt;
					var  xhr   = self.get_xhr_get(url, params);

					xhr.send();

					destroyIframe = true;
				}

				if ( destroyIframe ) {
					var iframeElement = document.getElementById(self.iframe_refresh_token_id);
					if (iframeElement) {
						iframeElement.remove();
					}
					return;
				}
			},

			/**
			 * Create Iframe to get new user session
			 *
			 * @param {object} userData
			 * @return {void}
			 */
			create_refresh_iframe: function(userData) {
				var self        = pmc.subscription_v2;

				// No create iframe if we don't have user or jwt data or if we have the sub_action === loggedin in the URL
				if ( ! userData.user || ! userData.jwt || self.is_logged_in_action() ) {
					return ;
				}

				// The Authorization API response contains valid HTML/JS including a new JWT—and will fire this event via PostMessage to inform us of the new JWT
				window.addEventListener('message', self.listen_for_refresh_iframe_postmessage);

				// Create and insert new iframe
				var auth_refresh_iframe = document.createElement('iframe');

				auth_refresh_iframe.setAttribute('style', 'display:none;width:0;height:0');
				auth_refresh_iframe.setAttribute('id', self.iframe_refresh_token_id);
				auth_refresh_iframe.src = "https://api.pmc.com/authorization/token/refresh" + '?jwt=' + userData.jwt + '&ip=' + userData.user.ip.join();
				auth_refresh_iframe.referrerPolicy = 'origin';

				document.body.appendChild(auth_refresh_iframe);
			},

			/**
			 * Function to Authenticate user by IP address.
			 * @param {function} callback
			 * @return {void}
			 */
			ip_auth : function (callback) {
				var self   = pmc.subscription_v2;
				var params = '?action=pmc_authenticate_by_ip';
				var xhr    = self.get_xhr_get(self.ajax_url, params);

				// Setup our listener to process completed requests
				xhr.onload = function () {
					callback && callback(JSON.parse(xhr.response), xhr.status);
				};

				xhr.send();
			},

			/**
			 * Return xhr object to make an AJAX GET request
			 *
			 * @param {string} url
			 * @param {string} params
			 * @return {object} xhr
			 */
			get_xhr_get: function(url, params) {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;
				var xhr  = window.XMLHttpRequest ? new XMLHttpRequest() : new ActiveXObject('Microsoft.XMLHTTP');

				// Appended random string is used to prevent caching of the AJAX call responses
				xhr.open( "GET", url + params + '&r=' + self.get_random() );
				xhr.setRequestHeader( 'X-Requested-With', 'XMLHttpRequest' );

				return xhr
			},

			/**
			 * Return session data
			 */
			get_session_data: function () {
				try {
					return pmc.subscription_v2.subscriber_data.session;
				} catch ( e ) {
					Rollbar.warn( 'Failed get_session_data', { 'error': e } );
					return {};
				}
			},

			/**
			 * Return `true` if user has session active.
			 *
			 * @return {boolean}
			 */
			has_session: function () {
				return 'true' === pmc.cookie.get('pmcsc_sub_has_session');
			},

			/**
			* Return `true` if the user has session data.
			*
			* @return {boolean}
			*/
			has_session_data: function( prop ) {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				if ( self.has_subscriber_data() && self.subscriber_data.hasOwnProperty( 'session' ) && self.subscriber_data.session ) {
					if ( 'undefined' !== typeof prop && '' !== prop ) {
						return self.subscriber_data.session.hasOwnProperty( prop );
					}
					return true;
				}

				return false;
			},

			/**
			 * Return `true` if user has data
			 *
			 * @return {boolean}
			 */
			has_user: function () {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				return 'true' === pmc.cookie.get( 'pmcsc_sub_has_user' ) || self.is_admin_user || self.is_token_user;
			},

			/**
			* Return `true` if the user has user data
			*
			* @return {boolean}
			*/
			has_user_data: function( prop ) {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				if ( self.has_subscriber_data() && self.subscriber_data.hasOwnProperty( 'user' ) && self.subscriber_data.user ) {
					if ( 'undefined' !== typeof prop && '' !== prop ) {
						return self.subscriber_data.user.hasOwnProperty( prop );
					}
					return true;
				}

				return false;
			},

			/**
			 * Return `true` if unknownip cookie is true
			 *
			 * @return {boolean}
			 */
			has_unknownip: function () {
				return 'true' === pmc.cookie.get( 'pmcsc_sub_unknownip' );
			},

			/**
			 * Return `true` if user has site license
			 *
			 * @return {boolean}
			 */
			has_site_license: function () {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				if ( self.has_user_data( 'site_license' ) ) {
					if (
						self.subscriber_data.user.site_license.hasOwnProperty( 'salesforce_account_id' ) &&
						self.subscriber_data.user.site_license.hasOwnProperty( 'user_ip' )
						) {
						return self.subscriber_data.user.site_license.salesforce_account_id !== '' && self.subscriber_data.user.site_license.user_ip !== '';
					}
				}

				return false;
			},

			/**
			 * Return `true` if user has entitlement for fallback function ( older version i.e function without param `has_entitlements()` )
			 * Return `true` if user has entitlement(s)
			 *
			 * @param {array} entitlements    Entitlement to check from subscriber data entitlement.
			 * @param {string} condition      Expects `and` and `or` values for entitlements.
			 *
			 * @return {boolean}
			 */
			has_entitlements: function( entitlements, condition ) {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2,
				entitlements = ( undefined === entitlements ) ? [] : entitlements,
				condition = ( undefined === condition ) ? 'or' : condition;

				// If subscriber data has entitlement object.
				if ( self.has_user_data( 'entitlements' ) ) {

					/**
					 *  - If no entitlement are passed, it would act as fallback for already used previous version of this function .ie( `has_entitlements()` ) .
					 *  - Would check if array passed by user and subscriber entitlement data are not empty.
					 *  - Would only accept array as its first param.
					 */
					if ( entitlements.length > 0 && Array.isArray( entitlements ) && self.subscriber_data.user.entitlements.length > 0 ) {

						// Condition Only to excepts `and` and `or` condition, other values would be treated as `or`.
						if ( 'and' === condition ) {

							// Return true if every element of `entitlements` is present in `subscriber_data.user.entitlements`.
							return entitlements.every( function ( value ) {
								return ( self.subscriber_data.user.entitlements.indexOf( value ) >= 0 );
							} );
						} else {

							// Return true if any element of `entitlements` is present in `subscriber_data.user.entitlements`.
							return entitlements.some( function ( value ) {
								return (self.subscriber_data.user.entitlements.indexOf( value ) >= 0);
							} );
						}

					} else {
						return self.subscriber_data.user.entitlements.length > 0;
					}
				}

				return false;
			},

			/**
			* Return `true` is a user is concurrency restricted.
			*
			* @return {boolean}
			*/
			is_restricted: function() {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				if ( self.has_session_data( 'concurrency_restricted' ) ) {
					return self.subscriber_data.session.concurrency_restricted;
				}

				return false;
			},

			is_registered_user: function() {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				if ( self.has_user_data() && self.subscriber_data.user.acct.hasOwnProperty( 'reg' ) ) {
					if ( self.subscriber_data.user.acct.reg.hasOwnProperty( self.brands[self.brand_name] ) ) {
						var reg = self.subscriber_data.user.acct.reg[self.brands[self.brand_name]];

						if ( reg.hasOwnProperty( 'cam' ) && reg.hasOwnProperty( 'date' ) ) {
							return ( reg.cam > 0 ) && ( reg.date.match(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/).length > 0 );
						}
					}
				}

				return false;
			},

			get_registered_user_data: function() {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				return self.subscriber_data.user.acct.reg[self.brands[self.brand_name]];
			},

			/**
			 * Show/hide links depending of the current user status
			 *
			 * @return {void}
			 */
			render_links: function () {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				// Check if the theme will take care of rendering these links.
				// If so, exit early so those changes aren't overwritten.
				if (self.render_links_from_theme) {
					return;
				}

				var show_or_hide_element = function(selector, show_element) {
					var element = document.querySelector(selector);
					if (element) {
						var display = show_element ? '' : 'none';
						element.style.display = display;
					}
				};

				var is_logged_in_user = self.has_user() && self.has_session();

				// Show logout button if user is already logged in link and hide logout
				if ( is_logged_in_user && ! self.is_logged_out_action() ) {

					// Remove class `user-not-logged-in` if user is logged in for subscription links container
					var subscriptionLinks = document.querySelector('.subscription-links');
					if ( subscriptionLinks ) {
						subscriptionLinks.className = subscriptionLinks.className.replace('user-not-logged-in', '');
					}

					// Show user name and set logout session id
					var givenNameNode = document.querySelector('.subscriber-name .replace-username');
					var logoutElements = document.querySelectorAll('.subscriber-logout-link');

					if (givenNameNode) {
						givenNameNode.innerText = self.subscriber_data.user.given_name;
					}

					if (logoutElements) {
						logoutElements.forEach( function(element) {
							element.href = element.href + '&session-id=' +  self.subscriber_data.session.session_id;
						});
					}

					// Show and hide links
					show_or_hide_element('.subscriber-name', true);

					show_or_hide_element('.subscribe-link', false);

					document.querySelectorAll('.subscriber-login-link').forEach( function(element){
						element.style.display = 'none';
					});

					if ( ! self.has_site_license() ) {
						show_or_hide_element('.subscriber-logout-link', true);
						show_or_hide_element('.subscriber-self-care-link', true);
					}
				} else {
					// Show "Subscribe" and "Login" links
					show_or_hide_element('.subscribe-link', true);

					document.querySelectorAll('.subscriber-login-link').forEach( function(element){
						element.style.display = '';
					});

					// Send log to rollbar when user clicks login link
					document.querySelectorAll( "[href^='" + self.login_link + "']" ).forEach( function ( element ) {
						element.addEventListener( 'click', function ( event ) {
							var href = this.getAttribute( 'href' );
							try {
								event.preventDefault();
								Rollbar.debug( 'User clicked subscriber-login-link', function () {
									window.location.href = href;
								} );
							} catch ( e ) {
								window.location.href = href;
							}
						} );
					} );
				}
			},

			/**
			 * Determine if the subscriber data object is empty.
			 *
			 * @returns {boolean}
			 */
			has_subscriber_data: function () {
				return Object.keys(this.subscriber_data).length > 0;
			},

			/**
			 * Determine if we have logged out action
			 *
			 * @returns {boolean}
			 */
			is_logged_in_action: function () {
				var urlParams = pmc.subscription_v2.get_url_params();
				return 'logged_in' === urlParams.get('sub_action');
			},

			/**
			 * Determine if we have logged out action
			 *
			 * @returns {boolean}
			 */
			is_logged_out_action: function () {
				var urlParams = pmc.subscription_v2.get_url_params();
				return 'logged_out' === urlParams.get('sub_action');
			},

			/**
			 * Register a callback that fires when user data is done loading.
			 *
			 * Note: If user data is already loaded when this is called,
			 *       the callback is fired immediately.
			 *
			 * @param callback
			 * @param loggedOutCallback - Optional callback that fires immediately when the user is not logged in.
			 */
			on_subscriber_data_loaded: function (callback, loggedOutCallback) {
				loggedOutCallback = loggedOutCallback || function () {};

				// Trigger the callback immediately if user data has already been set.
				if (this.has_user() && this.has_subscriber_data()) {
					callback(this.subscriber_data);
					return;
				}

				// Trigger the logged out callback immediately if the user isn't logged in.
				if (! this.has_session()) {
					loggedOutCallback();
					return;
				}

				this.subscriber_data_listeners.push(callback);
			},

			/**
			 * Show concurrency message if the user has some restrictions.
			 */
			may_show_concurrency_restricted_modal: function(subscriber_data) {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				if (! self.is_paywall_content || ! self.is_single_post || ! self.has_session()) {
					return false;
				}

				if (subscriber_data && subscriber_data.session.concurrency_restricted) {
					var concurrencyText = "You are logged in to too many devices. Please log out of a device and reload this page.";
					var headerText      = "This log in is currently in use";

					var concurrencyModalId = 'pmc-subscription__concurrency-restricted-modal';

					var restrictedModalBodyElement = document.querySelector('#pmc-subscription__concurrency-restricted-modal-message');
					if (restrictedModalBodyElement) {
						restrictedModalBodyElement.innerText = concurrencyText;
					}

					var restrictedModalHeaderElement = document.querySelector('#pmc-subscription__concurrency-restricted-modal .modal__header h4');
					if (restrictedModalHeaderElement) {
						restrictedModalHeaderElement.innerText = headerText;
					}

					MicroModal.show(concurrencyModalId);
				}
			},

			/**
			 * Show account login modal when click account link
			 */
			may_show_account_login_modal: function(event) {
				var self                   = pmc.subscription_v2;
				var accountTypesForModal   = ['Agents', 'Corporate', 'Site License'];
				var userCurrentAccountType = self.subscriber_data.user.acct.type;

				if (accountTypesForModal.indexOf(userCurrentAccountType) !== -1 ) {
					event.preventDefault();

					var bodyText   = '';
					var headerText = '';

					switch (userCurrentAccountType) {
						case 'Agents':
							headerText = 'Contact customer service';
							bodyText = "For questions regarding your Rolling Stone Digital subscription, please email customerservicedigital@rollingstone.com or call 855-259-6134 (US and Canada) \/ 332-232-0115 (International).";
							break;
						case 'Corporate':
						case 'Site License':
							headerText = 'Contact your corporate administrator';
							bodyText   = "Need help contacting your corporate administrator regarding your Rolling Stone Digital access? Please email customerservicedigital@rollingstone.com or call 855-259-6134 (US and Canada) \/ 332-232-0115 (International).";
							break;
					}

					var accountLoginModal = 'pmc-subscription__account-login-modal';

					var accountLoginModalBodyElement = document.querySelector('#pmc-subscription__account-login-message');
					if (accountLoginModalBodyElement) {
						accountLoginModalBodyElement.innerText = bodyText;
					}

					var accountLoginModalHeaderElement = document.querySelector('#pmc-subscription__account-login-header');
					if (accountLoginModalHeaderElement) {
						accountLoginModalHeaderElement.innerText = headerText;
					}

					MicroModal.show(accountLoginModal);
				}
			},

			/***
			 * Show verify Identity Modal
			 */
			may_show_verify_identity_modal: function() {
				var self = pmc.subscription_v2;

				// Only show the verify modal to non-SL users without a session
				if ( self.has_session() || self.has_site_license() || self.is_admin_user || self.is_token_user ) {
					return;
				}

				var dismiss_link = document.getElementById( 'pmc-subscription__verify-identity-dismiss' );
				if ( dismiss_link ) {
					dismiss_link.addEventListener( 'click', self.delete_subscriber_cookie );
				}

				// Only show the verify modal on paid content
				if ( ! self.is_paywall_content || ! self.is_single_post ) {
					return;
				}

				MicroModal.show( 'pmc-subscription__verify-identity-modal' );
			},

			/**
			 * Fires any listeners once subscriber data is loaded.
			 */
			trigger_user_data_listeners: function () {
				var self = this;

				if (self.subscriber_data_listeners.length === 0) {
					return;
				}

				if (! self.has_subscriber_data()) {
					console.error('User data listeners triggered, but no user data exists.');
					return;
				}

				self.subscriber_data_listeners.forEach(function (callback) {
					callback(self.subscriber_data)
				});

				// Clear listeners
				self.subscriber_data_listeners = [];
			},

			/**
			 * Allows a theme to override link rendering
			 */
			override_rendering_links: function() {
				var self = this;
				self.render_links_from_theme = true;
			},

			/**
			 * Call callback function when window is loaded or if already loaded
			 */
			window_load_event: function(callback) {
				if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
					callback();
				} else {
					window.addEventListener("load", callback);
				}
			},

			/**
			 * Show subscriber error modal if we have an issue in the login process
			 */
			may_show_subscriber_error_modal: function() {
				var self        = pmc.subscription_v2;
				var urlParams   = self.get_url_params();

				var subErrorText      = urlParams.get('sub_error');
				var hasSubActionError = 'error' === urlParams.get('sub_action');

				if (hasSubActionError && (subErrorText && '' !== subErrorText)) {
					var modalBodyElement = document.querySelector('#pmc-subscription__subscriber-error-message');
					if (modalBodyElement) {
						modalBodyElement.innerText = "For assistance, please contact Customer Service at customerservicedigital@rollingstone.com, 855-259-6134 (US and Canada) or 332-232-0115 (International).";
					}

					var modalHeaderElement = document.querySelector('#pmc-subscription__subscriber-error-modal .modal__header h4');
					if (modalHeaderElement) {
						modalHeaderElement.innerText = subErrorText;
					}

					var subscriberErrorModalId = 'pmc-subscription__subscriber-error-modal';

					MicroModal.show(subscriberErrorModalId);
				}
			},

			/**
			 * Delete subscriber cookie and refresh page
			 */
			delete_subscriber_cookie: function( event ){
				// delete cookie before make the logout request to our authorization api service
				// this method is also used by the verify modal to destroy all user cookies
				if ( ! this.getAttribute( 'data-logout-action' ) ) {
					event.preventDefault();

					var currentElement = this;
					var self           = pmc.subscription_v2;
					var url            = self.ajax_url;
					var params         = '?action=pmc_delete_subscriber_cookie_ajax_callback';
					var xhr            = self.get_xhr_get( url, params );

					xhr.onload = function () {
						var response   = JSON.parse( this.response );
						var session_id = self.get_url_params( currentElement.href ).get( 'session-id' );

						if ( 'undefined' === typeof session_id || '' === session_id ) {
							Rollbar.warn( 'Logout URL missing session-id', { session: self.get_session_data() } );
							return;
						}

						if ( 200 !== this.status || true !== response.success ) {
							Rollbar.warn( 'Logout AJAX failed', {
								session: self.get_session_data(),
								xhrStatus: this.status,
								xhrStatusText: this.statusText,
								xhrResponse: response,
								xhrResponseURL: this.responseURL
							} );
							return;
						}

						currentElement.setAttribute( 'data-logout-action', true );

						try {
							Rollbar.info( 'User logged out', {
								has_session_data: self.has_session_data(), session_id: session_id }, function () {
								currentElement.click();
							} );
						} catch ( e ) {
							currentElement.click();
						}
					};

					return xhr.send();
				}
			},

			get_url_params: function( url ) {
				var queryString = '';

				if ( 'undefined' === typeof url || '' === url ) {
					queryString = window.location.search;
				} else {
					var splitUrl = url.split( '?' );
					if ( splitUrl[1] ) {
						queryString = splitUrl[1];
					}
				}

				if ( 'URLSearchParams' in window ) {
					return new URLSearchParams( queryString );
				} else {
					return {
						'get': function() {
							return '';
						}
					};
				}
			},

			/**
			 * Set body class for different user state.
			 * - Adds subscription user,entitlements and session classes to body element.
			 */
			set_body_class: function() {

				// 1. Setting user class.
				if ( this.has_user() ) {
					document.body.classList.add( 'pmc-subscription-has-user' );
				}

				// 2. Setting user entitlement class.
				if ( this.has_entitlements() ) {

					this.subscriber_data.user.entitlements.forEach( function( entitlement ) {
						document.body.classList.add( 'pmc-subscription-user-entitlement-' + entitlement.replace(".", "_").toLowerCase() );
					} );

				}

				// 3. Setting user session class.
				if ( this.has_session() ) {
					document.body.classList.add( 'pmc-subscription-user-has-session' );
				}

			},

			/**
			 * Initialization for event listening and data
			 *
			 * @return {void}
			 */
			init: function() {
				var self = this;

				self.window_load_event(function() {
					self.set_body_class();
					self.may_show_subscriber_error_modal();

					document.querySelectorAll('.subscriber-logout-link').forEach( function(element){
						element.addEventListener('click', self.delete_subscriber_cookie);
					});
				});

				if (self.has_user() && ! self.is_logged_out_action() ) {

					self.get_cookie_data(function (response, status) {
						if (200 === status && response.success) {
							self.subscriber_data = response.data;
							self.trigger_user_data_listeners();

							// We need to be sure to have subscriber_data and that the HTML is loaded to render links
							self.window_load_event(function(){
								self.render_links();
								self.create_refresh_iframe(self.subscriber_data);
								self.may_show_concurrency_restricted_modal(self.subscriber_data);
								self.may_show_verify_identity_modal();

								var self_care_link = document.querySelector('.subscriber-self-care-link');
								if ( self_care_link ) {
									self_care_link.addEventListener('click', self.may_show_account_login_modal);
								}
							});
						} else {
							Rollbar.warn( 'Subscriber data fetch failed', {
								session: self.get_session_data(),
								xhrStatus: status,
								xhrResponse: response
							} );
						}
					});
				} else {
					self.window_load_event(function(){
						self.render_links();
					});
				}

				if ( self.is_ip_auth_enabled && ! self.has_unknownip() && ! self.has_user() && ! self.is_logged_in_action() ) {
					self.ip_auth( function ( response, status ) {
						if ( 200 === status && response.success ) {
							try {
								var user = JSON.parse( decodeURIComponent( pmc.cookie.get( 'pmcsc_sub_reporting_data' ) ) ) || {};
								var acct = user.acct || {};
								var entitlements = user.entitlements.length > 0 ? user.entitlements.join( ',' ) : false;

								Rollbar.info( 'User authenticated by IP Auth', {
									sf_account_id: acct.acct_id || false,
									sf_contact_id_id: acct.contact_id || false,
									entitlements: entitlements
								} );
							}catch(e){}

							window.location.href = window.location.href + "?sub_action=logged_in";
						}
					});
				}
			}
		};

		pmc.subscription_v2.init();
  </script>
  <link href="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/cropped-rs-favicon.png?w=32" rel="icon" sizes="32x32"/>

  <script>
   function PMC_RS_isSectionOpen ( name ) {
				var storage = localStorage.getItem( 'PMC_RS_homeState' );
				var hasState = storage && 'undefined' !== typeof JSON.parse( storage )[ name ];
				return hasState ? JSON.parse( storage )[ name ] : true;
			}

			function PMC_RS_setHomeAppearance ( name ) {
				var isSectionOpen = PMC_RS_isSectionOpen( name );
				var section = document.querySelector( '[data-section="' + name +  '"]' );

				if ( null !== section ) {
					if ( isSectionOpen ) {
						section.classList.remove( 'is-closing' );
						section.classList.remove( 'is-closed' );
					} else {
						section.classList.add( 'is-closing' );
						section.classList.add( 'is-closed' );
					}
				}
			}

			function PMC_RS_toggleHomeAd ( name ) {
				var isSectionOpen = PMC_RS_isSectionOpen( name );
				var ad = document.querySelector( '[data-section-ad="' + name +  '"]' );

				if ( ! isSectionOpen && null !== ad ) {
					ad.parentNode.removeChild( ad );
				}
			}
  </script>

            <header class="c-gallery-card__header">
             <h4 class="c-gallery-card__headline t-bold">
              Inside Nick Cave’s Retrospective Photo Book, ‘Stranger Than Kindness’
             </h4>
             <p class="c-gallery-card__lead t-copy">
              A new book, Stranger Than Kindness, lifts the long black veil on what makes Nick Cave […]
             </p>
             <div class="c-gallery-card__thumbs">
              <figure class="c-gallery-card__thumb">
               <div class="c-crop c-crop--ratio-3x2">
                <img alt="&lt;p&gt;Influenced by David Bowie and the Sensational Alex Harvey Band, Nick Cave in costume and make-up, prancing on stage, was joined by his more subdued friends Phill Calvert, Chris Coyne, John Cocivera, Howard (last name unknown), Mick Harvey, and Brett Purcell in a group established while students at Caulfield Grammar. Performing at school socials such as those hosted by Korowa Girls’ School, along with church halls, the band – then unnamed and driven to gigs by members’ parents – performed covers and some original material.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;After completing their Higher School Certificates and launching themselves into art school, hairdressing and the public service, Cave, Calvert, and Harvey came back together and were joined by Tracy Pew, and later Rowland S. Howard, to form the Boys Next Door in 1977.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="c-crop__img" data-src="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/MM_154208.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90" data-srcset="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/MM_154208.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90 90w, https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/MM_154208.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=180 180w" height="60" sizes="90px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" width="90"/>
               </div>
               <!-- .c-crop -->
              </figure>
              <!-- .c-gallery-card__thumb -->
              <figure class="c-gallery-card__thumb">
               <div class="c-crop c-crop--ratio-3x2">
                <img alt="&lt;p&gt;Anita Lane and Cave wrote “From Her to Eternity” together. “Ah wanna tell you about a girl,” Cave begins. A girl who haunts the song’s speaker. “The desire to possess her is a wound.” Cave met Lane in 1977, when they were both at art school in Melbourne and Lane lived with her progressive parents and older brother. Besides “Stranger Than Kindness” and “From Her to Eternity,” Lane also contributed lyrics to “A Dead Song,” “Dead Joe,” and “Kiss Me Black,” using the exquisite corpse method, by passing a piece of paper back and forth, trading lines. The couple split in 1983 but they continue to keep in touch.&lt;/p&gt;
" class="c-crop__img" data-src="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Loan-820.86.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90" data-srcset="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Loan-820.86.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90 90w, https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Loan-820.86.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=180 180w" height="60" sizes="90px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" width="90"/>

Mick, for example, became my chief collaborator, completely indispensable, for twenty years, and Phill, well, I always had a real soft spot for Phill, he was a lovely guy, but his drumming was ultimately at odds with what the band wanted to do, I think.”&lt;/p&gt;

            <header class="c-gallery-card__header">
             <h4 class="c-gallery-card__headline t-bold">
              The Rolling Stone Essentials of The Month: The Best Products We Tried and Tested in March 2021
             </h4>
             <p class="c-gallery-card__lead t-copy">
              Our editors round up their favorite products to buy this month, from surprisingly useful tech accessories to a homegrown CBD brand that delivers actual results
             </p>
             <div class="c-gallery-card__thumbs">
              <figure class="c-gallery-card__thumb">
               <div class="c-crop c-crop--ratio-3x2">
                <img alt='&lt;p&gt;Andover Audio’s SpinBase is an ingenious all-in-one audio system for anyone who wants to play records. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The flat, rectangular speaker is designed to sit just below a record player. It has an integrated phono preamp, so it can be used with modern and vintage turntables, and allows you to have a full turntable setup that takes up about as much space as a modern game console. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;I was skeptical at first, but the SpinBase delivers clear sound, even at loud volumes. You can adjust the bass and treble by twisting knobs on the back to get the mix just right for your ears or the album you’re spinning. The large volume knob on the front also acts as the power switch: Turn it all the way to the left, and the speaker shuts down. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;If you’ve written off vinyl because you don’t have enough space for a full audio system, Andover Audio’s SpinBase should make you reconsider. Purchase: &lt;a href="https://www.amazon.com/Andover-Audio-Spinbase-Turntable-Speaker/dp/B08GL3TC99?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rollingston07-20&amp;linkId=ed3da1bb24fa29775fe337b1d69d9e36&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl" target="_blank"&gt;$299 at Amazon.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
' class="c-crop__img" data-src="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Andover-Audio-Spinbase-Turntable-Speaker-System.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90" data-srcset="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Andover-Audio-Spinbase-Turntable-Speaker-System.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90 90w, https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Andover-Audio-Spinbase-Turntable-Speaker-System.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=180 180w" height="60" sizes="90px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" width="90"/>
               </div>
               <!-- .c-crop -->
              </figure>
              <!-- .c-gallery-card__thumb -->
              <figure class="c-gallery-card__thumb">
               <div class="c-crop c-crop--ratio-3x2">
                <img alt='&lt;p&gt;Wireless charging is fast, but I still plug my iPhone into a fast charging power adapter with a Lightning to USB-C cable when I’m short of time. This method can recharge a battery up to 50% in a half-hour. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;My new go-to cable is Anker’s Powerline III Flow, a colorful, ultra-flexible cable that Anker says has a “25,000-bend lifespan.” The cable feels pleasantly soft, and is malleable enough to snake around all of the other tech on my desk without showing signs of wear. &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;I’ve used Anker’s cables regularly for almost five years, and always had a good experience. If you’re settling for a cable that’s frayed, or patched with electrical tape, this is an upgrade you’ll appreciate every day. Purchase: &lt;a href="https://www.amazon.com/Anker-Powerline-Lightning-Certified-Supports/dp/B08H89QD4H?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rollingston07-20&amp;linkId=acdef5f9686189ba37e94f319049637a&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl" target="_blank"&gt;$24.99 at Amazon.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
' class="c-crop__img" data-src="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Anker-Powerline-III-Flow.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90" data-srcset="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Anker-Powerline-III-Flow.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90 90w, https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Anker-Powerline-III-Flow.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=180 180w" height="60" sizes="90px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" width="90"/>
               </div>
               <!-- .c-crop -->
              </figure>
              <!-- .c-gallery-card__thumb -->
              <figure class="c-gallery-card__thumb">
               <div class="c-crop c-crop--ratio-3x2">
                <img alt='&lt;p&gt;The world of CBD can be difficult to navigate – what’s a CBD tincture vs. CBD oil? How “high” will I get from using the products? What other benefits should I get from using CBD?&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;With a ton of information — and CBD brands — out there, we like the simplicity and accessibility of Cornbread Hemp. The Kentucky-based brand uses USDA-certified organic hemp extracts sourced exclusively from their home state to create products that help with everything from rest to recovery.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The easiest product to get into is their CBD Lotion. Rub a quarter-sized amount between your hands and massage the lotion into sore joints and muscles for rapid relief. We’ve even used CBD lotion on our achy feet after a long run or hike. Cornbread Hemp makes a &lt;a href="https://cornbread.pxf.io/oeRQYn" target="_blank"&gt;cooling methol formula&lt;/a&gt; to help soothe, and we like their &lt;a href="https://cornbread.pxf.io/zag1Ye" target="_blank"&gt;CBD lotion for dry skin&lt;/a&gt;, to help repair dry patches and keep our hands and body moisturized. Purchase: &lt;a href="https://cornbread.pxf.io/oeRQYn" target="_blank"&gt;$49.99 at Cornbread Hemp&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
' class="c-crop__img" data-src="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cornbread-hemp-lotion.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90" data-srcset="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cornbread-hemp-lotion.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90 90w, https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/cornbread-hemp-lotion.jpg?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=180 180w" height="60" sizes="90px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" width="90"/>

            <header class="c-gallery-card__header">
             <h4 class="c-gallery-card__headline t-bold">
              The Best Fitness Gifts to Give Someone Who Never Misses a Workout
             </h4>
             <p class="c-gallery-card__lead t-copy">
              From gifts for runners to presents for someone who's feeling a little sore after leg day, we’ve compiled a few of the coolest gift ideas for the active person in your life
             </p>
             <div class="c-gallery-card__thumbs">
              <figure class="c-gallery-card__thumb">
               <div class="c-crop c-crop--ratio-3x2">
                <img alt='&lt;p&gt;The coolest fitness gift of 2021? It’s tough to beat a fitness mirror, which features workouts led by trainers and, sometimes, includes weights and other accessories.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;One of the &lt;a href="https://www.rollingstone.com/product-recommendations/smart-home/best-fitness-mirror-reviews-1064555/" target="_blank"&gt;best fitness systems&lt;/a&gt; you can buy is the Tempo Studio. That’s why we’ve called it “&lt;a href="https://www.rollingstone.com/product-recommendations/smart-home/best-fitness-mirror-reviews-1064555/" target="_blank"&gt;the current champion of the fitness mirror game&lt;/a&gt;” (while the brand notes it’s not technically a mirror).&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;It’s built with a storage cabinet and everything from weight plates and a barbell to dumbells, a heart rate monitor and even an exercise mat, so you have everything you need to do any workout. What sets Tempo apart from other options is how it can help you adjust your form during exercises with its built-in sensors. It’s like your trainer’s right there with you during your workouts so you’re still getting the advice you need while you’re at home.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;With the $39 monthly membership, you can choose from both live or recorded strength and HIIT classes, to ones focused on mobility and recovery.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Purchase: &lt;a href="https://imp.i277339.net/c/256585/814975/11505?subId1=RS-&amp;u=https%3A%2F%2Ftempo.fit%2F%3F" target="_blank"&gt;$1,781 with discount code rollingstone214 (regularly $1,995) on Tempo Fit&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
' class="c-crop__img" data-src="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Tempo-Studio.png?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90" data-srcset="https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Tempo-Studio.png?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=90 90w, https://www.rollingstone.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Tempo-Studio.png?crop=3:2,smart&amp;w=180 180w" height="60" sizes="90px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" width="90"/>

                <img alt='&lt;p&gt;Whether you want to do sprints or take a cardio workout class, this ProForm treadmill includes iFit-hosted classes you can access on the Pro’s 22-inch high-definition touchscreen. Below its screen, the tread features a fan to keep you cool, and you can sync up your Bluetooth earbuds to hear your on-screen trainer. Think it’s too big of a gift to give? Think again — the Pro 9000’s SpaceSaver feature lets you fold the treadmill together when you’re not running. Best of all, a one-year iFit membership also comes with the Pro 9000, so it’s like you’re giving two gifts in one, high-tech package. Purchase: &lt;a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=87443X1590823&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.proform.com%2Ftreadmills%2Fpro9000%3F" target="_blank"&gt;$1,799, available at ProForm&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

       <p class="l-footer__newsletter-heading t-bold">
        Newsletter Signup
       </p>
       <div class="l-footer__newsletter-form">
        <form action="https://pages.email.rollingstone.com/signup-api/" class="c-form c-form--footer" method="POST">
         <div class="c-form__group">
          <div class="c-form__field t-semibold">
           <input name="Editorial_RollingStone_Opted_In" type="hidden" value="Yes"/>
           <input name="Editorial_RollingStone_Source" type="hidden" value="rs site"/>
           <input name="__contextName" type="hidden" value="FormPost"/>
           <input name="__executionContext" type="hidden" value="POST"/>
           <input class="js-newsletter-successpage" data-base-url="/signup?signup=success" name="__successPage" type="hidden" value="/signup?signup=success"/>
           <input class="js-newsletter-email c-form__input" name="EmailAddress" placeholder="Your email" required="" type="email"/>
           <script>
            jQuery( document ).ready(function($) {

	// Validate email will return true if valid and false if invalid.
	function validate_email( email ) {
		const expr = /^([\w.+-]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
		return expr.test( email );
	}

	$email_field = jQuery('.js-newsletter-email')
	$success_page_field = jQuery('.js-newsletter-successpage');

	if ( 0 === $email_field.length || 0 === $success_page_field.length ) {
		return;
	}

	success_page_base_url = $success_page_field.data( 'base-url' );

	$email_field.on( 'keyup blur', ( e ) => {

		// validate email and check for empty value.
		if ( '' === $( e.target ).val() || validate_email( $( e.target ).val() ) ) {
			$( e.target ).removeClass( 'invalid' );
		}

		var email_address = encodeURIComponent( $( e.target ).val() );
		$success_page_field.val( success_page_base_url + '&email=' + email_address );

	} );

});
           </script>
          </div>
          <!-- .c-form__field -->
          <button class="c-form__button c-form__button--black--bg">
           <span class="t-bold t-bold--upper">
            Submit
           </span>
          </button>
         </div>
         <!-- .c-form__group -->
        </form>

           <script>
            jQuery( document ).ready(function($) {

	// Validate email will return true if valid and false if invalid.
	function validate_email( email ) {
		const expr = /^([\w.+-]+)@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.)|(([\w-]+\.)+))([a-zA-Z]{2,4}|[0-9]{1,3})(\]?)$/;
		return expr.test( email );
	}

	$email_field = jQuery('.js-newsletter-email')
	$success_page_field = jQuery('.js-newsletter-successpage');

	if ( 0 === $email_field.length || 0 === $success_page_field.length ) {
		return;
	}

	success_page_base_url = $success_page_field.data( 'base-url' );

	$email_field.on( 'keyup blur', ( e ) => {

		// validate email and check for empty value.
		if ( '' === $( e.target ).val() || validate_email( $( e.target ).val() ) ) {
			$( e.target ).removeClass( 'invalid' );
		}

		var email_address = encodeURIComponent( $( e.target ).val() );
		$success_page_field.val( success_page_base_url + '&email=' + email_address );

	} );

});
           </script>
